## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Apache Beam Pipeline Runner Translation Layer

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/beam under runners/core-java/ and runners/core-construction-java/ that translate a Beam pipeline graph into runner-specific execution primitives. Identify: the PipelineTranslator interface, the TransformHierarchy walker, the PTransformOverride mechanism, the ExecutableStagePayload construction, and the BoundedSource/UnboundedSource adapter classes. For each file report its path and key class name.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/beam--v2.62.0.

432026-03-08T20:15:11.293518agentmessage-
The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary of Findings

### 1. PipelineTranslator Interface/Abstract Class
There is no single canonical `PipelineTranslator` interface in the core; each runner defines its own:
- **`FlinkPortablePipelineTranslator`** (`runners/flink/.../FlinkPortablePipelineTranslator.java`) — the primary portable pipeline translator **interface** for Flink
- **`FlinkPipelineTranslator`** — abstract base class for Flink translators
- **`SparkPipelineTranslator`** / **`SparkPortablePipelineTranslator`** — Spark translator interfaces
- **`PipelineTranslator`** (Spark Structured Streaming) — abstract class
- **`PipelineTranslation`** (`sdks/java/core/.../construction/PipelineTranslation.java`) — core utility converting Pipeline ↔ RunnerApi.Pipeline proto

### 2. TransformHierarchy Walker
- **`TransformHierarchy`** (`sdks/java/core/.../sdk/runners/TransformHierarchy.java`) — maintains the tree of applied PTransforms and provides the visitor/walker mechanism

### 3. PTransformOverride Mechanism
- **`PTransformOverride`** — pairs a matcher with a factory to replace transforms
- **`PTransformOverrideFactory`** — interface for producing replacement transforms
- **`PTransformMatcher`** — predicate interface identifying transforms to replace
- **`PTransformMatchers`** — factory methods for common matchers

### 4. ExecutableStagePayload Construction
- **`ExecutableStage`** (interface) — defines `toPayload()` building the `ExecutableStagePayload` proto
- **`ImmutableExecutableStage`** — concrete implementation
- **`ExecutableStageTranslation`** — extracts `ExecutableStagePayload` from transforms
- **`GreedyStageFuser`** / **`GreedyPipelineFuser`** — fuse transforms into executable stages

### 5. BoundedS
